<div id="review_2970501291" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2970501291" />
    <a title="Ines" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43642795-ines"><img alt="Ines" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542692123p2/43642795.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2970501291?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ines" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ines" href="/user/show/43642795-ines">Ines</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2970501291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3996637581312905724">I immediately say that I loved the book and my rating is on a 3.80*<br/>I like books where from the very first pages you are taken with a noose neck of anxiety and tension and you can not do anything but turn endlessly the pages to discover the unfolding of the plot... This book has just about everything of this kind, a woman in one piece who finds herself catapulted into a chasm of pain and violence caused by her husband a real serial killer,. Gina/Gwen is presented very well by Caine, her character</span>
  <span id="freeText3996637581312905724" style="display:none">I immediately say that I loved the book and my rating is on a 3.80*<br>I like books where from the very first pages you are taken with a noose neck of anxiety and tension and you can not do anything but turn endlessly the pages to discover the unfolding of the plot... This book has just about everything of this kind, a woman in one piece who finds herself catapulted into a chasm of pain and violence caused by her husband a real serial killer,. Gina/Gwen is presented very well by Caine, her character immediately captures you, surely for me, she managed to have my sympathy. First weak and succubed woman and then transformed for survival into a strong, tenacious and calculating one, always calculating every steps to be taken on.<br>She is renewed in the tenacious will and strength to keep her children alive from the destruction created by the father.<br>Even her kids, Connor/bradi and Lennie/Lily, are well characterized, each with their own attitude, weaknesses and uniqueness. This is absolutly a story to be read in one breath, maybe I even chose to read it after a series of challenging and exhausting readings, but the plot is very special, we already know everything at the start, there are not the classic culprits to be found, no... here everything is already served on a plate.<br>The supporting structure of the plot holds up, what instead scrapes and slows the flight towards a higher rating for this book, are the small facets that deposited one above the other, that gradually create little credibility to the entire history; ( the car that destroys the garage right where lies dead a victim of her husband, Absalom and his help to Gwen as hacker, the characters of Cade and Javier.... absolutely a little thrown there just to make the meatloaf's stuffing).<br>However do not be frightened by my moderate evaluation,this is a thriller that deserves......I say right away that took me in anxiety much more' than the Kim Stone's series by Angela Marsons!!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1568695336i/28158403._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Dico subito che il libro mi è piaciuto un sacco e la mia valutazione è su un 3,80*<br>Mi piacciono i libri dove già nelle prime pagine vieni preso con un cappio al collo di ansia e tensione e non si puo far altro che girare senza fine le pagine per scoprire lo svolgersi della trama....Questo libro ha proprio tutto del genere, una donna tutto d'un pezzo che si ritrova catapultata in una voragine di dolore e violenza causata da un marito serial killer. Gina/Gwen viene presentata molto bene dalla Caine, il suo personaggio ti cattura subito, sicuramente per me, è riuscita ad avere la mia simpatia. Prima donna debole e succube e poi trasformata per sopravvivenza in una donna forte, tenace e calcolatrice di ogni minimo passo da compiere, rinnovata nella tenace volontà e forza di far sopravvivere i suoi figli dalla distruzione creata dal padre ... anche i suoi figli, Connor/Bradi e Lennie/Lily, sono ben caratterizzati, ognuno con la sua attitudine, debolezze ed unicità. Una storia che si legge tutta d'un fiato, forse ho anche scelto di leggerlo dopo una serie di letture impegnative e spossanti, ma la trama è particolarissima, sappiamo già tutto in partenza, non vi sono i classici colpevoli da scovare, no... qui tutto è già servito su di un piatto. La struttura portante della trama regge, quello che invece raschia e rallenta il volo verso una valutazione piu' alta di questo libro sono le piccole sottigliezze che depositate una sopra l'altra creano pian piano poca credibilità all'intera storia; ( la macchina che distrugge il garage proprio nel punto dove giace morta una vittima del marito, Absalom e il suo aiuto come hacker, il personaggio di Cade e di Javier.... assolutamente un pò buttati lì giusto per fare da ripieno del polpettone)<br>Comunque non fatevi spaventare dalla mia valutazione morigerata, è un thriller che merita......dico subito che mi ha preso in ansia molto di piu' rispetto alla serie di Kim Stone della Marsons!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3996637581312905724" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('8qePNZ9cjxOFuQn0W7OZJgt1VilmSAN31gSamvvlCJPIgebnJAJGeyKSvZWsRpP53Sqx4ajFjRCNetwrNqb6CQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/sSMbudXmGr13Hb3AQe6JL3mqtMjQH+2vjNPjR94u5nE4uW8XAlRAlL3wpb28rD7a7lNG+3N8dHlTQk80jtJAw==')})
  }
